╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk authoring`

```

 Usage: mdk authoring [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Evolve an agent through the typed, reversible authoring catalog (ADR 025): add contexts, edit
 instructions, set models, ingest KB, add skills/evals — each planned, validated, and undoable. The
 conversational copilot lands in a later release; this is the scriptable spine.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ list      List the authoring action catalog (self-describing).                                   │
│ plan      Dry-run an action: show its diff + estimate + confirmation gate (NO writes).           │
│ apply     Checkpoint → apply → verify an action. Confirmation-gated for risky ones.              │
│ undo      Revert the last applied action to its pre-action checkpoint.                           │
│ history   Print the authoring action log (oldest-first).                                         │
│ audit     Show the append-only authoring audit log (every plan/apply/undo, D7e).                 │
│ replay    Re-apply the recorded *applied* action sequence through the driver (D7e).              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk authoring apply`

```

 Usage: mdk authoring apply [OPTIONS] ACTION

 Checkpoint → apply → verify an action. Confirmation-gated for risky ones.

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    action      TEXT  Action name (see `mdk authoring list`). [required]                        │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --args                        TEXT  JSON object of the action's args.                            │
│ --project  -p                 PATH  Project root.                                                │
│ --yes      -y                       Confirm a cost/networked/destructive action.                 │
│ --fast                              Auto-apply additive+reversible+free actions without          │
│                                     prompting.                                                   │
│ --verify       --no-verify          Run validate + mock-run after apply (D3). [default: verify]  │
│ --help                              Show this message and exit.                                  │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk authoring audit`

```

 Usage: mdk authoring audit [OPTIONS]

 Show the append-only authoring audit log (every plan/apply/undo, D7e).

 Distinct from the live undo stack (``history``): this is the immutable
 record of what the copilot did, when, and at what cost. A corrupt/missing
 log degrades to a warning + whatever could be read — it never crashes.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --project  -p      PATH  Project root.                                                           │
│ --output   -o      TEXT  'text' (default) or 'json'. [default: text]                             │
│ --help                   Show this message and exit.                                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk authoring history`

 Usage: mdk authoring history [OPTIONS]

│ --output   -o      TEXT  'text' (default) or 'json'. [default: text]                             │
│ --help                   Show this message and exit.                                             │

 Usage: mdk authoring plan [OPTIONS] ACTION

 Dry-run an action: show its diff + estimate + confirmation gate (NO writes).

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    action      TEXT  Action name (see `mdk authoring list`). [required]                        │

│ --help                   Show this message and exit.                                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk authoring replay`

```

 Usage: mdk authoring replay [OPTIONS]

 Re-apply the recorded *applied* action sequence through the driver (D7e).

 SAFETY: every step is re-driven through the SAME plan → confirm → apply →
 verify spine as a live edit — never a raw re-write — so the D2 confirmation
 gate + D3 verify (revert-on-failure) + D4 checkpoint/undo all hold. Gated
 steps prompt (or require ``--yes``); a failing step is reported and the
 replay continues.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --project  -p      PATH  Project root.                                                           │
│ --yes      -y            Confirm gated (cost/networked/destructive) steps.                       │
│ --fast                   Auto-apply additive+reversible+free steps without prompting.            │
│ --help                   Show this message and exit.                                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk authoring undo`

```

 Usage: mdk authoring undo [OPTIONS]

 Revert the last applied action to its pre-action checkpoint.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --project  -p      PATH  Project root.                                                           │
│ --help                   Show this message and exit.                                             │

### `mdk batch submit`

```

 Usage: mdk batch submit [OPTIONS] AGENT DATASET.JSONL

 Submit a JSONL dataset as a batch of async runs.

 Examples:

 # Fire-and-forget against the active target
 $ mdk batch submit faq-agent prompts.jsonl
 → prints {"batch_id": "...", "total": 42, "status": "queued"}

 # Wait for the whole batch to finish
 $ mdk batch submit faq-agent prompts.jsonl --wait

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    agent        TEXT           Agent name registered on the target runtime. [required]         │
│ *    dataset      DATASET.JSONL  Path to a JSONL dataset — one JSON object per line = one run's  │
│                                  input.                                                          │
│                                  [required]                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --target         -t      TEXT          Deployment target name (from `mdk config list-targets`).  │
│                                        Omit to use the active target.                            │
│ --wait           -w                    Block until every row reaches a terminal state, then      │
│                                        print the aggregate.                                      │
│ --timeout                FLOAT         Max seconds to wait when --wait is set. After this the    │
│                                        batch continues server-side; CLI exits 124.               │
│                                        [default: 600.0]                                          │
│ --poll-interval          FLOAT         Seconds between batch-status polls (--wait only).         │
│                                        [default: 2.0]                                            │
│ --notify-email           TEXT          Email the worker notifies as EACH row reaches a terminal  │
│                                        status.                                                   │
│ --output         -o      [table|json]  [default: table]                                          │
│ --help                                 Show this message and exit.                               │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk bench`

```

 Usage: mdk bench [OPTIONS] PATH INPUT

 Benchmark an agent across multiple models (cost / latency / quality).

 Examples:

 # Use bench.models from movate.yaml + agent's evals/judge.yaml
 $ movate bench ./faq-agent "What is movate?"

 # Two specific models, no judge — just cost+latency
 $ movate bench ./faq-agent "hi" \
       -m openai/gpt-4o-mini-2024-07-18 \
       -m anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5-20251001

 # Inline rubric for freeform LLM-as-judge
 $ movate bench ./faq-agent --runs 3 --rubric "Is the answer concise and correct?"

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    path           PATH   Path to agent directory. [required]                                   │
│      input_arg      INPUT  Input: a plain string (auto-wraps to the agent's single required      │
│                            string field), JSON object, file path, or '-' for stdin.              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --input        -i      TEXT                   Alternative way to pass input (preferred for       │
│                                               explicit JSON).                                    │
│ --model        -m      TEXT                   Provider to test. Repeatable. Defaults to          │
│                                               bench.models from movate.yaml.                     │
│ --judge        -j      TEXT                   Judge provider for quality scoring. Defaults to    │
│                                               bench.judges[0] from movate.yaml.                  │
│ --rubric               TEXT                   Inline scoring rubric. Required for LLM-as-judge   │
│                                               if judge.yaml has none.                            │
│ --rubric-file          PATH                   Path to a rubric file (overrides --rubric).        │
│ --runs         -r      INTEGER                Runs per model. Use 3+ to smooth latency/cost      │
│                                               variance.                                          │
│                                               [default: 1]                                       │
│ --gate-mode            TEXT                   Score aggregation across N runs: mean | min | p10. │
│                                               [default: mean]                                    │
│ --mock                                        Use the deterministic MockProvider (no API keys).  │
│ --output       -o      [table|json|markdown]  Output format: table (default) | json | csv.       │
│                                               [default: table]                                   │
│ --help                                        Show this message and exit.                        │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk benchmark`

```

 Usage: mdk benchmark [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Shadow-replay past runs against a candidate model. mdk benchmark live is the MVP.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ live   Shadow-replay past runs against a candidate model.                                        │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk benchmark live`

```

 Usage: mdk benchmark live [OPTIONS] AGENT

 Shadow-replay past runs against a candidate model.

 Pulls recent successful runs from storage, re-executes each with
 --candidate-model overriding the agent's
 ``model.provider``, and renders a side-by-side comparison.

 No production impact: we never call the candidate on
 live traffic — only on RunRecords already persisted.

 Examples:

   $ mdk benchmark live triage \
       --candidate-model anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5-20251001
   $ mdk benchmark live triage --candidate-model X --limit 50 \
       --since-days 7
   $ mdk benchmark live triage --candidate-model X --mock

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      AGENT  Agent name or path. [required]                                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --candidate-model        TEXT     LiteLLM-style model string to test against the recorded     │
│                                      runs (e.g. openai/gpt-4o-mini-2024-07-18).                  │
│                                      [required]                                                  │
│    --limit                  INTEGER  How many recent successful runs to replay. Max 200.         │
│                                      [default: 20]                                               │
│    --since-days             INTEGER  Only replay runs from the last N days. 0 = no time filter.  │
│                                      [default: 0]                                                │
│    --tenant-id              TEXT     Tenant scope for the storage lookup.                        │
│    --mock                            Use MockProvider for the candidate — hermetic CI / offline. │
│    --json                            Emit the summary + per-row results as JSON.                 │
│    --help                            Show this message and exit.                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk canary`

```

 Usage: mdk canary [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Manage champion/challenger canary rollouts (ADR 016 D3).

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ set       Set (or update) an agent's canary rollout.                                             │
│ status    Show an agent's current canary config.                                                 │
│ compare   Compare live quality champion-vs-challenger (feedback + run/error counts).             │
│ promote   Promote a version to champion (assisted — concludes the canary).                       │
│ off       Kill switch: route 100% to champion (weight 0), or --delete the canary.                │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk canary compare`

```

 Usage: mdk canary compare [OPTIONS] AGENT

 Compare live quality champion-vs-challenger (feedback + run/error counts).

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    agent      TEXT  Agent to compare champion vs challenger for. [required]                    │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --challenger        TEXT                   Override the challenger version (default: from the    │
│                                            canary).                                              │
│ --champion          TEXT                   Override the champion version (default: from the      │
│                                            canary).                                              │
│ --format            [table|json|markdown]  [default: table]                                      │
│ --help                                     Show this message and exit.                           │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk canary set`

```

 Usage: mdk canary set [OPTIONS] AGENT

 Set (or update) an agent's canary rollout.

 Examples:

 # Send 10% of traffic to version 2026.5.23.1
 $ mdk canary set faq-agent --challenger 2026.5.23.1 --weight 10

 # Auto-promote once the challenger clears a 0.9 thumbs-up rate
 $ mdk canary set faq-agent --challenger 2026.5.23.1 --weight 25 \
     --auto-promote --eval-gate 0.9

 # Kill switch — back to 100% champion instantly
 $ mdk canary off faq-agent

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    agent      TEXT  Agent to roll out a canary for. [required]                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --challenger                               TEXT                     Challenger version to     │
│                                                                        receive canary traffic.   │
│                                                                        [required]                │
│    --weight         -w                        INTEGER RANGE            Percent of traffic        │
│                                               [0<=x<=100]              (0-100) routed to the     │
│                                                                        challenger. 0 = kill      │
│                                                                        switch.                   │
│                                                                        [default: 0]              │
│    --sticky             --no-sticky                                    Consistent routing per    │
│                                                                        thread (no                │
│                                                                        champion↔challenger flip  │
│                                                                        mid-conversation).        │
│                                                                        [default: sticky]         │
│    --champion                                 TEXT                     Pin the champion to a     │
│                                                                        specific version.         │
│                                                                        Default: registry latest. │
│    --auto-promote                                                      Opt-in: auto-promote the  │
│                                                                        challenger once it clears │
│                                                                        --eval-gate.              │
│    --eval-gate                                FLOAT                    Min challenger quality    │
│                                                                        (0-1) for auto-promote.   │
│                                                                        Required with             │
│                                                                        --auto-promote.           │
│    --auto-rollback      --no-auto-rollback                             Opt-in: a drift           │
│                                                                        regression on the         │
│                                                                        challenger auto-trips the │
│                                                                        kill switch (weight → 0). │
│                                                                        Default off = alert-only  │
│                                                                        (ADR 016 D5).             │
│                                                                        [default:                 │
│                                                                        no-auto-rollback]         │
│    --disabled                                                          Create the canary but     │
│                                                                        leave it dormant (routes  │
│                                                                        to champion).             │
│    --format                                   [table|json|markdown]    [default: table]          │
│    --help                                                              Show this message and     │
│                                                                        exit.                     │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk catalog submit`

```

 Usage: mdk catalog submit [OPTIONS] SLUG

 Submit a tenant-private catalog entry from ``<from-dir>``.

 Examples:

 # Publish a local agent dir as a private catalog entry
 $ mdk catalog submit returns-bot --from-dir ./agents/returns-bot \
     --title "Returns Bot" --shape rag_qa --tag support

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    slug      TEXT  Catalog entry slug (URL-safe id). [required]                                │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --from-dir                 PATH  Local directory; tarballed and uploaded as the entry bundle. │
│                                     [required]                                                   │
│    --name                     TEXT  Display name. Defaults to the slug.                          │
│    --title                    TEXT  Card title. Defaults to the slug.                            │
│    --description              TEXT  Plain-text description.                                      │
│    --tag                      TEXT  Tag to attach (repeatable).                                  │
│    --shape                    TEXT  ADR 028 shape (faq / rag_qa / ...).                          │
│    --recommended-for          TEXT  One-line use-case statement.                                 │
│    --version                  TEXT  [default: 0.1.0]                                             │
│    --target           -t      TEXT                                                               │
│    --help                           Show this message and exit.                                  │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk catalog sync`

```

 Usage: mdk catalog sync [OPTIONS]

 Trigger a manual catalog sync.

 v1's server-side handler is a STUB — it logs the intent and bumps
 the watermark. The production wiring against ``catalog.movate.io``
 is a separate Movate-side build (ADR 041 D4).

 Examples:

   # Pull the latest Movate-published entries
   $ mdk catalog sync --source movate

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --source          TEXT  Namespace to sync. Only 'movate' is meaningful in v1. [default: movate]  │
│ --target  -t      TEXT                                                                           │
│ --help                  Show this message and exit.                                              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk chat`

```

 Usage: mdk chat [OPTIONS] PATH

 Interactive REPL bound to one agent.

 Example:

   # Iterate on a prompt without retyping `movate run` each turn
   $ movate chat ./agents/faq-agent
   you> what is movate?
   ✦ movate is a declarative platform for AI agents and workflows...
   you> what's the alternative?
   ✦ Compared to writing agents in raw LangChain, movate gives you...
   you> :q

 Conversation memory is ON by default — each turn sees the prior
 user/assistant exchange so follow-ups like "what's the alternative?"
 resolve correctly. Pass ``--no-memory`` to make every turn
 independent (useful when iterating on a prompt and you DON'T want
 context bleeding between attempts).

 Each turn runs through the full executor (input validation,
 schema check, persistence) — exactly like ``movate run`` — so
 every message persists to local sqlite for ``movate trace replay``.

 Memory is in-process only — it lives for the duration of one
 chat session and is dropped on exit. Persisted conversations across
 sessions are a follow-up.

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    path      PATH  Path to an agent directory. [required]                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --no-stream          Disable streaming (wait for the full response, then render).                │
│ --no-memory          Disable conversation memory — each turn runs as a fresh one-shot.           │
│ --mock               Use the deterministic MockProvider (smoke / offline).                       │
│ --help               Show this message and exit.                                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk ci`

```

 Usage: mdk ci [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 CI helpers — pre-flight gates that wrap multi-agent invocations.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ eval   Eval every agent in the project; fail on any regression.                                  │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk ci eval`

```

 Usage: mdk ci eval [OPTIONS]

 Eval every agent in the project; fail on any regression.

 Examples:

 # Local pre-flight (same gate CI runs)
 $ movate ci eval --mock

 # In CI — append the diff summary to GitHub's PR view
 $ movate ci eval --mock --summary-file "$GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY"

 # Real-LLM eval with provider keys in env
 $ movate ci eval --runs 3 --regression-tolerance 0.05

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --baselines-dir                 PATH     Root dir under which each agent's baseline is           │
│                                          ``<dir>/<agent_name>/baseline.json``. Default: the      │
│                                          project's .mdk/ (or legacy .movate/).                   │
│ --regression-tolerance          FLOAT    Allowable score drop vs baseline before flagging a      │
│                                          regression. 0.0 means any drop fails; raise to ~0.05    │
│                                          for noisy LLM-as-judge.                                 │
│                                          [default: 0.0]                                          │
│ --runs                  -r      INTEGER  Runs per case (3+ for LLM-as-judge variance).           │
│                                          [default: 1]                                            │
│ --mock                                   Use the deterministic MockProvider (no API keys).       │
│ --summary-file                  PATH     Append a markdown summary to this file. Designed for    │
│                                          ``$GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY`` — set ``--summary-file         │
│                                          $GITHUB_STEP_SUMMARY`` in CI to get a rendered diff on  │
│                                          every PR.                                               │
│ --help                                   Show this message and exit.                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk compose`

```

 Usage: mdk compose [OPTIONS] NAME

 Scaffold a multi-agent workflow.yaml from a list of agents.

 Each --agents entry becomes one node; consecutive
 entries are wired with sequential edges. The generated file uses
 the linear workflow IR (Sprint M baseline); conditional routing
 / parallel / HITL land as the engine matures (Sprint U+).

 Examples:

   $ mdk compose customer-flow --agents triage,summarise,respond
   $ mdk compose returns --agents validate,fraud-check,approve [/dim]
       --runtime langgraph
   $ mdk compose flow --agents a,b --output workflows/x/flow.yaml

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      TEXT  Workflow name. Used as directory + spec.name. [required]                    │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --agents               TEXT  Comma-separated agent names to wire in sequence (e.g. --agents      │
│                              triage,summarise,respond).                                          │
│ --runtime              TEXT  Workflow runtime. native (default) uses the movate workflow IR.     │
│                              langgraph marks the workflow for the LangGraph compiler (scaffold   │
│                              today; full engine in Sprint U+).                                   │
│                              [default: native]                                                   │
│ --description  -d      TEXT  One-line workflow description recorded in spec.description.         │
│ --output       -o      TEXT  Where to write the workflow.yaml. Default:                          │
│                              workflows/<name>/workflow.yaml under project root.                  │
│ --force        -f            Overwrite OUTPUT if it already exists.                              │
│ --help                       Show this message and exit.                                         │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk config`

```

 Usage: mdk config [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Manage user-level movate config (deployment targets, active target).

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ add-target      Register a deployment target.                                                    │
│ list-targets    Show all registered targets, highlighting the active one.                        │
│ current         Print the active target as a single line (script-friendly).                      │
│ use             Set the active target — CLI commands default to it when --target is omitted.     │
│ set             Set a user-level config key (writes ``~/.movate/config.yaml``).                  │
│ show            Dump the resolved config (useful for debugging).                                 │
│ remove-target   Delete a target. If it was active, the active pointer is cleared                 │
│                 (next CLI call will require --target until you `config use` again).              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk config add-target`

```

 Usage: mdk config add-target [OPTIONS] NAME

 Register a deployment target.

 Examples:

 # Local dev runtime (no deploy config)
 $ mdk config add-target local --url http://127.0.0.1:8000 --key-env MDK_LOCAL_KEY

 # Prod, with deploy enabled, and make it the default
 $ mdk config add-target prod \
       --url https://movate-prod-api.eastus2.azurecontainerapps.io \
       --key-env MDK_PROD_KEY \
       --azure-subscription "$SUBSCRIPTION_ID" \
       --azure-resource-group movate-prod-rg \
       --azure-acr movateprodacr \
       --azure-env prod \
       --set-active

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      TEXT  Friendly target name, e.g. 'prod', 'staging'. [required]                    │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --url                         TEXT  Base URL of the runtime. [required]                       │
│ *  --key-env                     TEXT  Name of the env var that holds the bearer token (e.g.     │
│                                        MDK_PROD_KEY).                                            │
│                                        [required]                                                │
│    --set-active                        Make this the default target (saves you a `config use`    │
│                                        step).                                                    │
│    --azure-subscription          TEXT  Azure subscription id. Required to enable `movate deploy  │
│                                        --target <name>`.                                         │
│    --azure-resource-group        TEXT  Resource group containing the ACA env + ACR (e.g.         │
│                                        movate-dev-rg).                                           │
│    --azure-acr                   TEXT  ACR registry name without the .azurecr.io suffix (e.g.    │
│                                        movatedevacr).                                            │
│    --azure-env                   TEXT  Environment label (dev / staging / prod). Used to derive  │
│                                        Container App names: movate-{env}-api,                    │
│                                        movate-{env}-worker. Should match the `env` param used    │
│                                        when running the Bicep deployment.                        │
│    --azure-keyvault              TEXT  Key Vault name (no FQDN, e.g. movate-dev-kv-mvt) holding  │
│                                        the `bootstrap-api-key` secret. When set, `mdk deploy`    │
│                                        recovers a missing/stale bearer by PULLING this           │
│                                        guaranteed-trusted key instead of minting a fresh one     │
│                                        in-pod (which a non-durable / multi-replica runtime may   │
│                                        not trust).                                               │
│    --help                              Show this message and exit.                               │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk config current`

```

 Usage: mdk config current [OPTIONS]

 Print the active target as a single line (script-friendly).

 Use in shell prompts ("which env am I pointing at?") or as a
 sanity check before a destructive op:

   $ mdk config current
   prod  https://movate-prod.azurecontainerapps.io  MDK_PROD_KEY

   $ if [ "$(mdk config current | awk '{print $1}')" = prod ]; then
         echo "refusing to run dev tooling against prod"
     fi

 No target configured / no active pointer → exit 1 with a short
 stderr message (distinct from "no config exists" since we don't
 want to surface implementation detail to scripts).

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk config set`

```

 Usage: mdk config set [OPTIONS] KEY VALUE

 Set a user-level config key (writes ``~/.movate/config.yaml``).

 Mirrors the layered-config pattern (ADR 022): this writes the
 persistent USER layer; a project's ``project.yaml`` and per-invocation
 flags still override it.

 Supported keys:

   scaffold.model      — default LLM that powers ``mdk init --llm``
                        (e.g. anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5-20251001).
                        Distinct from the generated agent's runtime model.
   copilot.budget_usd  — cap on LLM spend per ``mdk dev`` / autopilot
                        session (e.g. 0.50). The copilot warns near it
                        and refuses the next call once exceeded. ``--budget``
                        on ``mdk dev`` overrides this.

 Example:

   $ mdk config set scaffold.model anthropic/claude-haiku-4-5-20251001
   $ mdk config set copilot.budget_usd 0.50

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    key        TEXT  Config key in section.field form, e.g. scaffold.model. [required]          │
│ *    value      TEXT  Value to set. [required]                                                   │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk contexts`

```

 Usage: mdk contexts [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 List and inspect shared context files injected into agent prompts. See
 docs/adr/002-skills-and-contexts.md for the design.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ list     List all context files in the project.                                                  │
│ show     Print the full body of a context file.                                                  │
│ create   Create a new context file pre-filled with a minimal template.                           │
│ attach   Wire an existing context into an agent's ``contexts:`` list.                            │
│ detach   Remove a context from an agent's ``contexts:`` list.                                    │
│ remote   Manage the runtime's MANAGED contexts registry over the API (ADR 060). Needs --target.  │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk contexts attach`

```

 Usage: mdk contexts attach [OPTIONS] NAME

 Wire an existing context into an agent's ``contexts:`` list.

 The context must already exist (project-level or agent-local). Create
 one first with mdk contexts create.

 Examples:

   # Attach a shared project context to an agent
   $ mdk contexts attach policy --agent rag-qa

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      TEXT  Context name (stem, no extension) to wire in. [required]                    │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --agent    -a      TEXT  Agent whose agent.yaml gains the context. [required]                 │
│    --project  -p      PATH  Project root. Defaults to the current directory. [default: .]        │
│    --help                   Show this message and exit.                                          │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk contexts create`

```

 Usage: mdk contexts create [OPTIONS] NAME

 Create a new context file pre-filled with a minimal template.

 Creates ``contexts/<name>.md`` at the project level by default. With
 ``--agent <name>``, creates ``agents/<agent>/contexts/<name>.md`` AND
 wires it into that agent's ``agent.yaml`` ``contexts:`` list so it takes
 effect on the next run (pass ``--no-attach`` to skip the wiring).

 Examples:

   # Create a project-level context (shared; not auto-attached)
   $ mdk contexts create policy

   # Create + wire a context into one agent in a single step
   $ mdk contexts create grounded-rubric --agent rag-qa

   # Create agent-local but leave agent.yaml untouched
   $ mdk contexts create draft --agent rag-qa --no-attach

   # Overwrite an existing context
   $ mdk contexts create policy --force

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      TEXT  Name for the new context file (stem, no extension). [required]              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --agent      -a      TEXT  Create the context inside agents/<agent>/contexts/ instead of the     │
│                            project-level contexts/ directory. The agent directory must already   │
│                            exist.                                                                │
│ --project    -p      PATH  Project root. Defaults to the current directory. [default: .]         │
│ --force      -f            Overwrite the file if it already exists.                              │
│ --no-attach                Don't wire the new context into the agent's agent.yaml. Only          │
│                            meaningful with --agent (project-level contexts aren't tied to a      │
│                            single agent, so they're never auto-attached).                        │
│ --help                     Show this message and exit.                                           │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk contexts detach`

```

 Usage: mdk contexts detach [OPTIONS] NAME

 Remove a context from an agent's ``contexts:`` list.

 Leaves the context file on disk — only the wiring in agent.yaml is removed.

 Examples:

   $ mdk contexts detach policy --agent rag-qa

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      TEXT  Context name to remove from the agent. [required]                           │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --agent    -a      TEXT  Agent whose agent.yaml loses the context. [required]                 │
│    --project  -p      PATH  Project root. Defaults to the current directory. [default: .]        │
│    --help                   Show this message and exit.                                          │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk contexts list`

```

 Usage: mdk contexts list [OPTIONS]

 List all context files in the project.

 Shows project-level contexts (``contexts/`` dir) and per-agent
 contexts (``agents/<name>/contexts/``), along with which agents
 reference each project-level context by name.

 Examples:

   # List all contexts in the current project
   $ mdk contexts list

   # Show only contexts relevant to one agent
   $ mdk contexts list --agent rag-qa

   # Include a snippet preview of each file
   $ mdk contexts list --verbose

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --project  -p      PATH  Project root to scan. Defaults to the current directory. [default: .]   │
│ --agent    -a      TEXT  Filter to one agent's local + referenced project contexts. Omit to show │
│                          all.                                                                    │
│ --verbose  -v            Show the first few lines of each context file.                          │
│ --help                   Show this message and exit.                                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk contexts remote update`

```

 Usage: mdk contexts remote update [OPTIONS] NAME

 Publish a NEW version of a managed context (rows are immutable).

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      TEXT  Context name. [required]                                                    │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --file         -f      PATH          Markdown file whose body is the new version. [required]  │
│ *  --version              TEXT          New version (rows are immutable). [required]             │
│    --description  -d      TEXT                                                                   │
│    --target       -t      TEXT                                                                   │
│    --output       -o      [table|json]  [default: table]                                         │
│    --help                               Show this message and exit.                              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk costs`

```

 Usage: mdk costs [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Historical cost reports from recorded runs. mdk costs report summarises spend per agent /
 provider.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
