│ report   Summarise spend per agent or provider from recorded runs.                               │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk costs report`

```

 Usage: mdk costs report [OPTIONS]

 Summarise spend per agent or provider from recorded runs.

 Examples:

 $ mdk costs report                          # per-agent, all-time
 $ mdk costs report --by provider            # which model burns the most
 $ mdk costs report --since-days 7           # last week
 $ mdk costs report --agent triage           # one agent only
 $ mdk costs report --json | jq '.rollups'   # pipe to BI

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --by                      TEXT     Group rollups by agent (default) or provider. Provider rollup │
│                                    answers "which model is eating my budget?"                    │
│                                    [default: agent]                                              │
│ --agent           -a      TEXT     Filter to one agent (e.g. --agent triage).                    │
│ --tenant-id               TEXT     Filter to one tenant (omit for cross-tenant in single-tenant  │
│                                    deploys).                                                     │
│ --since-days              INTEGER  Only count runs from the last N days. 0 (default) = no time   │
│                                    filter. Use 7 / 30 for weekly / monthly views.                │
│                                    [default: 0]                                                  │
│ --limit                   INTEGER  Maximum runs to fetch from storage before aggregating. Bump   │
│                                    if your history is huge.                                      │
│                                    [default: 10000]                                              │
│ --highlight-over          FLOAT    Red-bar rows whose total spend exceeds this USD threshold.    │
│                                    0.0 (default) = no highlighting. Example: --highlight-over    │
│                                    1.0 flags any agent that's burned > $1.                       │
│                                    [default: 0.0]                                                │
│ --json                             Emit JSON instead of a Rich table — pipe to jq / BI tools.    │
│ --help                             Show this message and exit.                                   │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk demo`

```

 Usage: mdk demo [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Demo project scaffold + the dashboard 'wow pack' seeder.

 Run bare ('mdk demo') to scaffold a runnable FAQ project; 'mdk demo seed' to populate dashboards
 with synthetic telemetry.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ new      Generate a complete runnable demo project (FAQ agent + dataset).                        │
│ seed     Populate the runtime with realistic synthetic telemetry (the "wow pack").               │
│ clear    Purge ALL demo-seeded telemetry (and nothing else).                                     │
│ doctor   Confirm the Monday-demo environment is GO (run after ``mdk demo seed``).                │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk demo clear`

```

 Usage: mdk demo clear [OPTIONS]

 Purge ALL demo-seeded telemetry (and nothing else).

 Deletes exactly the rows whose ``tenant_id`` starts with demo-
 — the marker mdk demo seed stamps on every record it creates.
 Real telemetry (any tenant without the prefix) is never touched.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --target          TEXT  Logical environment name (prod-guard + summary only). [default: local]   │
│ --force                 Required to clear a target whose name looks like prod/production.        │
│ --yes     -y            Skip the confirmation prompt.                                            │
│ --help                  Show this message and exit.                                              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk demo doctor`

```

 Usage: mdk demo doctor [OPTIONS]

 Confirm the Monday-demo environment is GO (run after ``mdk demo seed``).

 A green/red checklist mirroring ``mdk doctor``: the knowledge graph has
 nodes, the dashboards have telemetry + insights, the sample agents are
 registered + valid (one voice-capable), and a workflow is present. Exits
 non-zero if any hard check fails, so a pre-demo script can gate on it.

 Examples:

   $ mdk demo doctor                 # readiness checklist
   $ mdk demo doctor --run-agents    # + a mock agent run

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --run-agents    --no-run-agents      Also materialize + load one sample agent bundle through the │
│                                      agent loader (the same path `mdk run`/`mdk eval` use) to    │
│                                      prove it's runnable end-to-end — schemas, prompt, and       │
│                                      runtime adapter all resolve. Offline, $0. Off by default to │
│                                      keep the check fast.                                        │
│                                      [default: no-run-agents]                                    │
│ --help                               Show this message and exit.                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk demo new`

```

 Usage: mdk demo new [OPTIONS] DIR

 Generate a complete runnable demo project (FAQ agent + dataset).

 The output is a self-contained directory you can ``cd`` into and
 run immediately:

   $ mdk demo
   $ cd demo-faq
   $ cp .env.example .env  # then add your API key
   $ mdk run faq '{"question": "What is Python?"}'
   $ mdk eval faq

 Different from mdk init: init scaffolds
 one empty agent into an existing project. demo creates
 a full project with a working agent, prompt, schemas, and a sample
 eval dataset — the 60-second hello-world.

 Examples:

   $ mdk demo                       # creates ./demo-faq/
   $ mdk demo my-first-agent        # custom directory name
   $ mdk demo --force               # overwrite existing
   $ mdk demo --dry-run             # preview only

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   directory      DIR  Directory to create the demo in (default: ./demo-faq). [default: demo-faq] │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --force    -f        Overwrite DIR if it already exists. Destructive — wipes the existing        │
│                      contents.                                                                   │
│ --dry-run            Show what would be created without writing.                                 │
│ --help               Show this message and exit.                                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk demo seed`

```

 Usage: mdk demo seed [OPTIONS]

 Populate the runtime with realistic synthetic telemetry (the "wow pack").

 Generates demo-tagged RunRecords, EvalRecords and
 FailureRecords across agents x tenants x time — varied cost/latency/tokens,
 a trending eval pass-rate with one agent drifting, and two
 injected anomalies (a cost spike + a latency regression after a deploy) so
 the anomaly + narrative dashboard panels have a story to tell.

 Pass --with-voice to also GENERATE voice-turn records (Deepgram
 STT + Cartesia TTS) alongside each successful run. These are generated +
 counted but not persisted yet (no voice_turns table on the
 StorageProvider Protocol) — the flag exercises the generation path until the
 voice-storage ADR lands.

 Safety. Every seeded row is tagged: its tenant_id starts with
 demo- and its input carries a __mdk_demo__ marker.
 mdk demo clear purges exactly those rows (runs, evals, failures,
 and voice turns). Seeding a target whose name contains
 prod/production is refused unless you pass
 --force.

 Examples:

   $ mdk demo seed                              # 6 agents, 3 tenants, 7 days
   $ mdk demo seed --with-voice                 # + voice-turn rows
   $ mdk demo seed --days 30 --with-voice       # 30-day history + voice
   $ mdk demo seed --agents 4 --days 14         # smaller fleet
   $ mdk demo seed --clear-first --seed 42      # reproducible reset

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --target                               TEXT                       Logical name of the            │
│                                                                   environment being seeded (used │
│                                                                   only for the prod-name safety  │
│                                                                   guard + the summary). The      │
│                                                                   actual storage backend is      │
│                                                                   selected by MOVATE_DB_URL /    │
│                                                                   MOVATE_DB as usual.            │
│                                                                   [default: local]               │
│ --agents       -a                      INTEGER RANGE [1<=x<=8]    Number of demo agents.         │
│                                                                   [default: 6]                   │
│ --tenants      -t                      INTEGER RANGE [1<=x<=6]    Number of demo tenants.        │
│                                                                   [default: 3]                   │
│ --days         -d                      INTEGER RANGE [1<=x<=120]  Days of history to span.       │
│                                                                   Defaults to 7 for a tight demo │
│                                                                   window. Use --days 30 for a    │
│                                                                   richer historical view.        │
│                                                                   [default: 7]                   │
│ --seed                                 INTEGER                    RNG seed — same seed           │
│                                                                   reproduces the same data.      │
│                                                                   [default: 1337]                │
│ --clear-first                                                     Purge existing demo data       │
│                                                                   before seeding.                │
│ --force                                                           Required to seed a target      │
│                                                                   whose name looks like          │
│                                                                   prod/production.               │
│ --with-voice                                                      Also GENERATE voice-turn       │
│                                                                   records (Deepgram STT +        │
│                                                                   Cartesia TTS) for each         │
│                                                                   successful run — realistic     │
│                                                                   latency/cost figures, same     │
│                                                                   seeded RNG. NOTE: these are    │
│                                                                   generated + counted but NOT    │
│                                                                   persisted yet (no voice_turns  │
│                                                                   table on the StorageProvider   │
│                                                                   Protocol); the flag exercises  │
│                                                                   the generation path until the  │
│                                                                   voice-storage ADR lands.       │
│ --full             --telemetry-only                               Also seed the demo SCENARIO —  │
│                                                                   sample agents (incl. one       │
│                                                                   voice-capable + one workflow)  │
│                                                                   and a Movate-themed knowledge  │
│                                                                   graph — so the registry, graph │
│                                                                   viewer, and playground light   │
│                                                                   up too, not just the           │
│                                                                   dashboards. Pass               │
│                                                                   --telemetry-only for the       │
│                                                                   historical telemetry-only      │
│                                                                   seed.                          │
│                                                                   [default: full]                │
│ --help                                                            Show this message and exit.    │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk deploy`

```

 Usage: mdk deploy [OPTIONS]

 Build the runtime image + roll out to Azure Container Apps.

 Examples:

   # Default — build + push + update both apps + verify
   $ movate deploy --target prod

   # CI fire-and-forget (don't block on /healthz)
   $ movate deploy --target prod --no-wait

   # Redeploy an existing image (rollback to prev sha)
   $ movate deploy --target prod --skip-build --image-tag movate:0.5.0-abc1234

   # Worker-only update (e.g. dispatch logic change)
   $ movate deploy --target prod --only worker

   # Plan the deploy without running it
   $ movate deploy --target prod --dry-run

 Requires:

   * ``az`` CLI installed and authenticated (``az login``).
   * Target registered with full Azure config:
     ``movate config add-target ... --azure-subscription ... --azure-resource-group ...
       --azure-acr ... --azure-env ...``

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --target                   -t                     TEXT   Deployment target (from `movate config  │
│                                                          list-targets`). Omit for active.        │
│ --image-tag                                       TEXT   Explicit image tag (e.g.                │
│                                                          movate:0.5.0-abc1234). Defaults to      │
│                                                          <version>-<git-sha-short>. Use to       │
│                                                          redeploy an existing image.             │
│ --skip-build                                             Don't run `az acr build`; just update   │
│                                                          Container Apps to --image-tag. Useful   │
│                                                          for rollbacks: --skip-build --image-tag │
│                                                          movate:0.5.0-prev_sha.                  │
│ --no-wait                                                Update Container Apps and exit          │
│                                                          immediately, without polling /healthz.  │
│                                                          CI fire-and-forget mode.                │
│ --wait-timeout                                    FLOAT  Max seconds to poll /healthz for the    │
│                                                          new version. Exits 124 on timeout.      │
│                                                          [default: 300.0]                        │
│ --dry-run                                                Print the `az` commands that would run; │
│                                                          don't execute.                          │
│ --skip-validate                                          Skip the validate-before-deploy         │
│                                                          guardrail. By default a runtime-mode    │
│                                                          deploy runs the same checks as mdk      │
│                                                          validate --all on the project in cwd    │
│                                                          and aborts before building/pushing any  │
│                                                          image if any agent or workflow fails.   │
│                                                          Use this to deploy a known-good image   │
│                                                          despite a transient validation issue    │
│                                                          (e.g. an env var only set in the        │
│                                                          deployed pod).                          │
│ --only                                            TEXT   Update only one Container App: 'api',   │
│                                                          'worker', or 'temporal-worker'. Default │
│                                                          rolls api + worker (and temporal-worker │
│                                                          when Temporal is enabled for the env).  │
│                                                          Useful when a code change is scoped to  │
│                                                          one app.                                │
│ --skip-image-parity-check                                Skip the post-update image-parity       │
│                                                          guard. By default, after rolling the    │
│                                                          Container Apps, mdk deploy reads the    │
│                                                          image back off movate-<env>-api,        │
│                                                          -worker, and (when Temporal is enabled) │
│                                                          -temporal-worker and fails loudly if    │
│                                                          they don't all match — a runtime        │
│                                                          feature that lands on one image but not │
│                                                          another (e.g. durable-HITL / ADR 080    │
│                                                          terminal-state sync, which must be on   │
│                                                          the WORKER image) silently no-ops       │
│                                                          otherwise. Pass this for an intentional │
│                                                          --only roll, or when the                │
│                                                          temporal-worker is rolled out-of-band   │
│                                                          (bicep / scripts/deploy-temporal.sh).   │
│ --notify                                                 On successful deploy, fire outbound     │
│                                                          notifications. Reads TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN │
│                                                          + TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID for a Telegram       │
│                                                          message, MOVATE_DEPLOY_WEBHOOK for a    │
│                                                          generic JSON POST                       │
│                                                          (Slack/Teams/Discord/custom). Both fire │
│                                                          if both are configured. Failures are    │
│                                                          non-fatal — deploy stays green.         │
│ --mode                                            TEXT   Deploy mode. runtime: build + roll the  │
│                                                          movate container image (requires        │
│                                                          Dockerfile in cwd — i.e. the movate-cli │
│                                                          source tree). agents: upload the        │
│                                                          customer agents under agents/*/ to the  │
│                                                          deployed runtime (requires project.yaml │
│                                                          in cwd or an ancestor; doesn't rebuild  │
│                                                          the image). auto (default): pick by     │
│                                                          what's in cwd — Dockerfile → runtime,   │
│                                                          project.yaml → agents.                  │
│                                                          [default: auto]                         │
│ --diff                                                   Preview what would change without       │
│                                                          uploading. Compares each local agent's  │
│                                                          agent.yaml hash against the deployed    │
│                                                          version and prints a table of new /     │
│                                                          changed / unchanged agents. Exits 0;    │
│                                                          nothing is uploaded. Only applies to    │
│                                                          agents-mode.                            │
│ --status                                                 List all live agents on the target      │
│                                                          runtime. Calls GET /api/v1/agents and   │
│                                                          renders a table of name / version /     │
│                                                          created-at. Nothing is deployed. Only   │
│                                                          applies to agents-mode.                 │
│ --no-auto-recover                                        Disable the 401 auto-recovery path.     │
│                                                          Default behavior: on a 401 from the     │
│                                                          runtime, mint a fresh key inside the    │
│                                                          Container App and retry once. Use this  │
│                                                          flag in CI or when debugging            │
│                                                          key-storage issues directly.            │
│ --with-kb                                                Agents-mode only. After a successful    │
│                                                          deploy, also ingest each deployed       │
│                                                          agent's bundled agents/<name>/kb/       │
│                                                          directory to the target runtime —       │
│                                                          deploy ships the prompt + contexts, but │
│                                                          the knowledge base is otherwise a       │
│                                                          separate mdk kb ingest step. Agents     │
│                                                          without a non-empty kb/ dir are         │
│                                                          skipped. No effect under --dry-run /    │
│                                                          --diff.                                 │
│ --smoke-test                   --no-smoke-test           Agents-mode only. After a successful    │
│                                                          deploy, dispatch ONE remote run of each │
│                                                          just-deployed agent against the target  │
│                                                          and show pass/fail + response + run_id  │
│                                                          + cost — proving the new behavior is    │
│                                                          live, not just that /healthz answers.   │
│                                                          Input comes from the first row of       │
│                                                          evals/dataset.jsonl (or, interactively, │
│                                                          a one-time prompt). Default: OFFER      │
│                                                          interactively in a terminal; SKIP       │
│                                                          non-interactively unless --smoke-test   │
│                                                          is passed. --no-smoke-test always       │
│                                                          skips. A failed smoke test warns but    │
│                                                          never fails the (already-succeeded)     │
│                                                          deploy.                                 │
│ --verbose                  -v                            Stream the az acr build log live during │
│                                                          the image build (runtime-mode).         │
│                                                          Default: show only a spinner + live     │
│                                                          elapsed timer (the raw layer/timing     │
│                                                          output isn't useful at deploy time).    │
│                                                          Use this to watch a slow or failing     │
│                                                          build in real time. All progress stays  │
│                                                          on stderr; the --json/stdout contract   │
│                                                          is unchanged.                           │
│ --force                                                  Agents-mode only. Overwrite skills that │
│                                                          already exist on the runtime. Without   │
│                                                          this flag a 409 is returned when a      │
│                                                          skill already exists, preventing silent │
│                                                          breakage on accidental re-deploy. Pass  │
│                                                          --force for intentional overwrites      │
│                                                          (e.g. bumping a skill's implementation  │
│                                                          without changing its name). CLI FLAG    │
│                                                          (additive): does not affect agent       │
│                                                          conflict policy.                        │
│ --help                                                   Show this message and exit.             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk dev`

```

 Usage: mdk dev [OPTIONS] [AGENT]

 Guided agent authoring: scaffold → edit → live-test → deploy.

 Examples:

 # Resume work on an existing agent, live-testing on every save
 $ mdk dev rag-qa

 # Scaffold a brand-new agent, then drop straight into the loop
 $ mdk dev support-bot --template faq

 # No API keys handy? Drive the loop with the mock provider
 $ mdk dev rag-qa --mock

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   agent      [AGENT]  Agent name or path. If it doesn't exist yet, dev offers to scaffold it.    │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --template          -t      TEXT     Template to scaffold from when the agent doesn't exist.     │
│                                      Defaults to 'default'.                                      │
│ --llm                       TEXT     Natural-language description — scaffold a new agent from it │
│                                      (LLM-generated).                                            │
│ --input             -i      TEXT     Test input for the live loop (plain string or JSON).        │
│                                      Defaults to the first row of evals/dataset.jsonl, or        │
│                                      prompts you once if there's no dataset.                     │
│ --mock                               Use the deterministic MockProvider for runs (no API keys    │
│                                      needed).                                                    │
│ --eval-sample-size          INTEGER  Eval-in-the-loop: after each live re-run, score the first N │
│                                      eval cases and show the mean-accuracy delta vs the previous │
│                                      run. 0 (default) = off — a fast quality signal while you    │
│                                      tune, capped to N cases. Honors --mock so the loop stays    │
│                                      free/offline.                                               │
│                                      [default: 0]                                                │
│ --target                    TEXT     Azure deploy target (from ~/.movate/config.yaml). Used by   │
│                                      the deploy action.                                          │
│ --budget                    FLOAT    Cap on cumulative LLM spend (USD) for this session's        │
│                                      copilot/autopilot calls. Warns near the cap, refuses the    │
│                                      next call once exceeded. Overrides `copilot.budget_usd` in  │
│                                      ~/.movate/config.yaml.                                      │
│ --poll-interval             FLOAT    Seconds between filesystem polls in the live loop.          │
│                                      [default: 0.5]                                              │
│ --runtime                   TEXT     Override the workflow execution backend (ADR 055 D3):       │
│                                      native (default), temporal, or langgraph. Precedence: this  │
│                                      flag > workflow.yaml 'runtime:' field > native. Read-only — │
│                                      never mutates the spec. Applies to workflow targets only;   │
│                                      agent dev ignores it. (The dev loop validates + evals; use  │
│                                      mdk run --runtime temporal <wf> to execute on the backend.) │
│ --help                               Show this message and exit.                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk diagnose`

```

 Usage: mdk diagnose [OPTIONS] [AGENT] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Diagnose recent failures for an agent — cluster + propose typed fixes (ADR 043 D1, read-only with
 respect to the agent).

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   agent      [AGENT]  Agent name registered on the target runtime.                               │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --window-days                              INTEGER       Lookback window in days. Failures older │
│                                                          than this are ignored.                  │
│                                                          [default: 30]                           │
│ --min-failures                             INTEGER       Cluster floor — clusters smaller than   │
│                                                          this are dropped from the result.       │
│                                                          [default: 5]                            │
│ --max-clusters                             INTEGER       Maximum clusters to return.             │
│                                                          [default: 10]                           │
│ --eval-failures      --no-eval-failures                  Include failing eval records as failure │
│                                                          signal.                                 │
│                                                          [default: eval-failures]                │
│ --drift              --no-drift                          Include drift detections (computed from │
│                                                          eval history) as signal.                │
│                                                          [default: drift]                        │
│ --canary             --no-canary                         Include failed runs on the canary       │
│                                                          challenger as signal.                   │
│                                                          [default: canary]                       │
│ --budget-usd                               FLOAT         Hard spend cap for the diagnoser's LLM  │
│                                                          call. Estimated > budget = error.       │
│                                                          [default: 1.0]                          │
│ --model                                    TEXT          Optional provider/model override (e.g.  │
│                                                          openai/gpt-4o-mini).                    │
│ --target         -t                        TEXT          Deployment target name (from `mdk       │
│                                                          config list-targets`). Omit to use the  │
│                                                          active target.                          │
│ --wait           -w                                      Block until the diagnose completes,     │
│                                                          then pretty-print the result.           │
│ --poll-interval                            FLOAT         Seconds between status polls (--wait    │
│                                                          only).                                  │
│                                                          [default: 1.0]                          │
│ --timeout                                  FLOAT         Max seconds to wait when --wait is set; │
│                                                          after this CLI exits 124.               │
│                                                          [default: 300.0]                        │
│ --output         -o                        [table|json]  [default: table]                        │
│ --help                                                   Show this message and exit.             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ show   Fetch + render a previously-submitted diagnose.                                           │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk diagnose show`
