 Usage: mdk diagnose show [OPTIONS] AGENT JOB_ID

 Fetch + render a previously-submitted diagnose.

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    agent       TEXT  Agent name (informational; resolution is by job_id). [required]           │
│ *    job_id      TEXT  The diagnose job id (from a prior `mdk diagnose`). [required]             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --target  -t      TEXT          Deployment target name. Omit to use the active target.           │
│ --output  -o      [table|json]  [default: table]                                                 │
│ --help                          Show this message and exit.                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk diff`

```

 Usage: mdk diff [OPTIONS] [SNAP_A] [SNAP_B]

 Compare two snapshots or the working tree against a git commit.

 Snapshot mode (mdk diff <a> <b>) — shows
 files added / removed / modified between two snapshots, plus agent +
 workflow count deltas. Answers "what changed between green-bar and
 red-bar?"

 Git mode (mdk diff --git) — shows files
 under the captured roots (agents/, movate.yaml,
 etc.) that differ between the working tree and the named git ref.
 Quick pre-commit drift check; no snapshot needed.

 Examples:

   # Snapshot vs snapshot (Sprint N original)
   $ mdk diff abc12345 def67890

   # Working tree vs last commit (Sprint Q extension)
   $ mdk diff --git

   # Working tree vs main
   $ mdk diff --git --ref main

   # CI gate — exit 1 if anything changed
   $ mdk diff old-baseline current && echo "no drift"

   # JSON for piping to jq
   $ mdk diff a b --json | jq '.files_modified[].path'

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   snap_a      [SNAP_A]  'Before' snapshot — full hash or short-hash prefix (≥4 chars). Omit when │
│                         using --git.                                                             │
│   snap_b      [SNAP_B]  'After' snapshot — full hash or short-hash prefix. Omit when using       │
│                         --git.                                                                   │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --git                    Compare the working tree against the last commit (or --ref) instead of  │
│                          two snapshots. Cheap drift check before committing.                     │
│ --ref              TEXT  Git ref to compare against in --git mode. Defaults to HEAD. Examples:   │
│                          main, release/v0.7, <commit-sha>.                                       │
│                          [default: HEAD]                                                         │
│ --project  -p      PATH  Project root. Defaults to walking up from cwd for movate.yaml.          │
│ --json                   Emit JSON instead of a Rich table — pipe-friendly for CI.               │
│ --all                    Include unchanged files in the table (off by default — diffs typically  │
│                          show only changes). Useful for audit trails that want the full picture. │
│ --help                   Show this message and exit.                                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk docs`

```

 Usage: mdk docs [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Auto-generated project documentation. mdk docs runbook generates a markdown ops runbook from the
 current project state — refresh after significant changes.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ runbook   Generate an ops runbook from the current project state.                                │
│ cli       Generate the full ``mdk`` CLI command reference.                                       │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk docs cli`

```

 Usage: mdk docs cli [OPTIONS] OUTPUT

 Generate the full ``mdk`` CLI command reference.

 Introspects the Typer app's underlying Click command tree and emits a
 markdown doc: the command tree, then each command's help + options.
 Pure introspection — no project state, no network — so it's safe in CI.

 Use ``--check`` in CI to fail the build if the committed reference has
 drifted from the live command surface.

 Examples:

   $ mdk docs cli                       # writes docs/cli-reference.md
   $ mdk docs cli --dry-run             # preview, no write
   $ mdk docs cli --check               # CI freshness gate

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   output      PATH  Where to write the reference (default: docs/cli-reference.md).               │
│                     [default: docs/cli-reference.md]                                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --check            CI mode: regenerate in memory and exit non-zero if OUTPUT is stale (or        │
│                    missing). Writes nothing.                                                     │
│ --dry-run          Print the generated markdown to stdout without writing.                       │
│ --help             Show this message and exit.                                                   │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk docs runbook`

```

 Usage: mdk docs runbook [OPTIONS] OUTPUT

 Generate an ops runbook from the current project state.

 The runbook captures: project metadata, every agent (with model +
 eval-dataset status), discovered env vars (required vs optional),
 common operation recipes, the state-cluster cheatsheet, and a
 troubleshooting section.

 Re-run after significant changes — the doc stays useful only as
 long as it matches reality.

 Examples:

   $ mdk docs runbook                          # writes docs/RUNBOOK.md
   $ mdk docs runbook --dry-run                # preview, no write
   $ mdk docs runbook ops/runbook.md --force   # custom location

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   output      PATH  Where to write the generated markdown (default: docs/RUNBOOK.md).            │
│                     [default: docs/RUNBOOK.md]                                                   │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --force    -f        Overwrite OUTPUT if it already exists.                                      │
│ --dry-run            Print the generated markdown to stdout without writing.                     │
│ --help               Show this message and exit.                                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk doctor`

```

 Usage: mdk doctor [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Environment + configuration sanity check. Default: project-wide doctor. Subcommand agent <name>
 focuses on one agent.

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --target         -t      TEXT  Also run the Azure preflight for a registered target (az login →  │
│                                subscription → RG → ACR → Container Apps → /healthz). Use this    │
│                                when `movate deploy` is failing.                                  │
│ --explain                      Per-check explanation block.                                      │
│ --licenses                     Print a per-dep SPDX license report.                              │
│ --no-fix-prompt                Skip the interactive `mdk fix?` prompt when issues are found.     │
│ --help                         Show this message and exit.                                       │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ agent   Agent-specific health check: validates, prices, smoke-tests.                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk doctor agent`

```

 Usage: mdk doctor agent [OPTIONS] AGENT

 Agent-specific health check: validates, prices, smoke-tests.

 Runs eight checks against one agent:

   1. agent.yaml + schemas load
   2. prompt template renders against the first dataset row
   3. model is in the packaged pricing table
   4. all declared skills resolve in the skill registry
   5. all declared contexts exist on disk
   6. evals/dataset.jsonl has at least one row
   7. eval baseline is committed (or hint to create one)
   8. last run from storage (if any) — recency + cost

 Ends with a greppable ``mdk_doctor_agent_summary:`` line for CI
 parity with the project-wide doctor's ``mdk_doctor_summary:``.

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    name      AGENT  Agent name (resolved under agents/<name>) or a literal path to an agent    │
│                       directory.                                                                 │
│                       [required]                                                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --project-root        PATH  Override the project root. Defaults to walking up from cwd.          │
│ --help                      Show this message and exit.                                          │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk eval`

```

 Usage: mdk eval [OPTIONS] [PATH]

 Run the eval suite for an agent and gate on a threshold.

 Examples:

 # Exact-match scoring against the dataset
 $ mdk eval ./faq-agent --gate 0.7

 # Compare against a stored (sqlite) baseline by id
 $ mdk eval ./faq-agent --baseline 4f8a-... --regression-tolerance 0.05

 # CI flow: gate against a git-tracked baseline file
 $ mdk eval ./faq-agent --mock --baseline-file .movate/baseline.json

 # Refresh the committed baseline on main-branch merge
 $ mdk eval ./faq-agent --mock --output-baseline .movate/baseline.json

 # Hermetic CI run (no API keys needed)
 $ mdk eval ./faq-agent --mock

 # Black-box eval against a deployed mdk runtime
 $ mdk eval https://faq-runtime.example.com \
     --agent-yaml ./faq-agent --api-key mvt_dev_...

 # Inside a project, bare names resolve to ./agents/<name>:
 $ mdk eval rag-qa --gate 0.7

 # Inline LLM judge — no judge.yaml needed:
 $ mdk eval ./ticket-triager \
     --judge-model anthropic/claude-opus-4-7 \
     --judge-rubric 'Score 0-1: 1=correct routing, 0=wrong' \
     --runs 3

 # NEW: LLM-generated cases + 10-category scorecard (opt-in):
 $ mdk eval ./rag-qa --scorecard
 $ mdk eval ./rag-qa --scorecard --scorecard-count 25 --scorecard-mix domain

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   path      [PATH]  Path to an agent directory OR a base URL of a deployed movate runtime        │
│                     (http://… or https://…). With a URL, each dataset case is submitted as a     │
│                     job, polled to terminal, and the resulting RunRecord is scored — no local    │
│                     provider is invoked. Requires --agent-yaml so the local copy provides the    │
│                     dataset and output schema for scoring. Omit with --all to sweep every agent  │
│                     in the current project.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --all                                                         Evaluate every agent under         │
│                                                               ./agents/ in the current project.  │
│                                                               Aggregates results into a summary  │
│                                                               table; exits non-zero if any agent │
│                                                               fails its gate. The CI eval-gate   │
│                                                               workflow uses this.                │
│ --gate                             FLOAT                      Per-case score required to pass    │
│                                                               (0.0-1.0).                         │
│                                                               [default: 0.7]                     │
│ --gate-mode                        TEXT                       How to aggregate N runs per case   │
│                                                               into a single score: mean | min |  │
│                                                               p10.                               │
│                                                               [default: mean]                    │
│ --runs                     -r      INTEGER                    Runs per case. Use 3+ for          │
│                                                               LLM-as-judge to defeat sampling    │
│                                                               variance.                          │
│                                                               [default: 1]                       │
│ --mock                                                        Use the deterministic MockProvider │
│                                                               (no API keys).                     │
│ --baseline                         TEXT                       Eval id of a stored EvalRecord to  │
│                                                               diff against. CLI exits 1 on       │
│                                                               regression.                        │
│ --baseline-file                    PATH                       Path to a JSON-serialized          │
│                                                               EvalRecord. CI-friendly            │
│                                                               alternative to --baseline since CI │
│                                                               runners have ephemeral sqlite.     │
│                                                               Mutually exclusive with            │
│                                                               --baseline.                        │
│ --output-baseline                  PATH                       Write the current EvalRecord to    │
│                                                               this path as JSON. Use on          │
│                                                               main-branch merges to refresh the  │
│                                                               committed baseline; CI then diffs  │
│                                                               PRs against it.                    │
│ --regression-tolerance             FLOAT                      Allowable score drop vs baseline   │
│                                                               before flagging a regression       │
│                                                               (0.0-1.0).                         │
│                                                               [default: 0.0]                     │
│ --objective                        TEXT                       Only run cases tagged for the      │
│                                                               named objective (id from           │
│                                                               agent.yaml: objectives). Gates on  │
│                                                               that objective's own threshold     │
│                                                               (declared in agent.yaml), not      │
│                                                               --gate. Use this in CI to fail PRs │
│                                                               that regress a specific objective  │
│                                                               while letting others slip — e.g.   │
│                                                               `--objective routing-accuracy`.    │
│ --output                   -o      [table|json|markdown]      [default: table]                   │
│ --api-key                          TEXT                       Bearer token for remote eval (path │
│                                                               starts with http(s)://). Falls     │
│                                                               back to the MDK_API_KEY env var    │
│                                                               (legacy MOVATE_API_KEY also        │
│                                                               accepted).                         │
│                                                               [env var: MDK_API_KEY,             │
│                                                               MOVATE_API_KEY]                    │
│ --agent-yaml                       PATH                       Local agent directory used for     │
│                                                               dataset + output schema when       │
│                                                               evaluating a deployed runtime.     │
│                                                               Required when path is a URL;       │
│                                                               ignored when path is a directory.  │
│ --guided                   -g                                 Interactive wizard: walks the      │
│                                                               operator through agent selection,  │
│                                                               provider (mock/real), gate,        │
│                                                               runs-per-case, and baseline        │
│                                                               behavior — then runs the resulting │
│                                                               eval. Auto-triggered when mdk eval │
│                                                               runs with no args from a TTY       │
│                                                               inside a project.                  │
│ --gate-faithfulness                FLOAT                      Minimum mean faithfulness score    │
│                                                               (0.0-1.0) required to pass. Only   │
│                                                               fires when the dataset has         │
│                                                               grounding fields. Exit 1 if        │
│                                                               faithfulness mean is below this    │
│                                                               threshold.                         │
│ --gate-coverage                    FLOAT                      Minimum mean coverage score        │
│                                                               (0.0-1.0) required to pass. Only   │
│                                                               fires when the dataset has         │
│                                                               expected_coverage fields. Exit 1   │
│                                                               if coverage mean is below this     │
│                                                               threshold.                         │
│ --gate-latency                     FLOAT                      Minimum mean latency score         │
│                                                               (0.0-1.0) required to pass. A      │
│                                                               score of 1.0 means every case      │
│                                                               completed within its budget;       │
│                                                               decays linearly to 0.0 at 2x the   │
│                                                               budget. Exit 1 if latency mean is  │
│                                                               below this threshold.              │
│ --gate-context-compliance          FLOAT                      Minimum mean context-compliance    │
│                                                               score (0.0-1.0) required to pass.  │
│                                                               Only fires when the agent has      │
│                                                               declared contexts and a judge      │
│                                                               model. Exit 1 if                   │
│                                                               context_compliance mean is below   │
│                                                               this threshold.                    │
│ --gate-refusal                     FLOAT                      Minimum mean refusal score         │
│                                                               (0.0-1.0) required to pass. Only   │
│                                                               fires when the dataset has         │
│                                                               refusal_expected rows (generated   │
│                                                               by mdk eval-gen --mode refusal).   │
│                                                               Score 1.0 when the agent refuses   │
│                                                               as expected, 0.0 when it complies. │
│                                                               Exit 1 if refusal mean is below    │
│                                                               this threshold.                    │
│ --gate-retrieval-accuracy          FLOAT                      Minimum mean retrieval-accuracy    │
│                                                               score (0.0-1.0) required to pass.  │
│                                                               Only fires when the agent has      │
│                                                               grounding context (contexts/ files │
│                                                               or dataset grounding fields) and a │
│                                                               judge model. Exit 1 if             │
│                                                               retrieval_accuracy mean is below   │
│                                                               this threshold.                    │
│ --compare                                                     Auto-compare against the previous  │
│                                                               run. Reads evals/.last-run.json as │
│                                                               the baseline (if it exists) and    │
│                                                               writes the current run there       │
│                                                               afterward. Shorthand for           │
│                                                               --baseline-file                    │
│                                                               evals/.last-run.json               │
│                                                               --output-baseline                  │
│                                                               evals/.last-run.json.              │
│ --variant                          TEXT                       Path to a second agent directory   │
│                                                               to run A/B comparison against.     │
│                                                               Runs the same dataset against both │
│                                                               agents and prints a side-by-side   │
│                                                               score table. The primary agent's   │
│                                                               gate still applies; the variant is │
│                                                               informational. Example: --variant  │
│                                                               agents/rag-qa-v2                   │
│ --judge-model                      TEXT                       LiteLLM model string for the       │
│                                                               LLM-as-judge, e.g.                 │
│                                                               anthropic/claude-opus-4-7.         │
│                                                               Overrides judge.yaml — no config   │
│                                                               file needed. Requires              │
│                                                               --judge-rubric. Repeat the flag    │
│                                                               twice or more for a multi-judge    │
│                                                               panel — judges score independently │
│                                                               and the panel mean is used unless  │
│                                                               std-dev exceeds the variance       │
│                                                               threshold, in which case           │
│                                                               --arbitrator-model (if set) breaks │
│                                                               the tie.                           │
│ --judge-rubric                     TEXT                       Scoring rubric passed verbatim to  │
│                                                               the LLM judge(s). Required when    │
│                                                               --judge-model is set. Example:     │
│                                                               'Score 0-1: 1=all fields correct,  │
│                                                               0=any field wrong'                 │
│ --arbitrator-model                 TEXT                       Tiebreaker model used when panel   │
│                                                               judges disagree by more than       │
│                                                               --variance-threshold. Pick a       │
│                                                               high-capability model from a       │
│                                                               family different from any panel    │
│                                                               judge. Only meaningful when 2+     │
│                                                               --judge-model are set.             │
│ --variance-threshold               FLOAT                      Std-dev threshold above which the  │
│                                                               arbitrator is consulted (0.0-1.0). │
│                                                               Lower = more sensitive to          │
│                                                               disagreement; default 0.3 catches  │
│                                                               roughly the 'mild divergence'      │
│                                                               case. Only used in panel mode.     │
│                                                               [default: 0.3]                     │
│ --scorecard                                                   Switch to the new LLM-generated    │
│                                                               test cases + 10-category scorecard │
│                                                               flow (same as mdk eval-scorecard). │
│                                                               Skips the dataset.jsonl-based      │
│                                                               scoring entirely; instead          │
│                                                               Anthropic generates                │
│                                                               --scorecard-count test inputs in   │
│                                                               the chosen --scorecard-mix and     │
│                                                               scores each against accuracy /     │
│                                                               faithfulness / format / safety /   │
│                                                               refusal / hallucination /          │
│                                                               completeness /                     │
│                                                               instruction_following / latency /  │
│                                                               cost. Other flags (--gate,         │
│                                                               --baseline, --runs, etc.) are      │
│                                                               ignored when --scorecard is set.   │
│ --scorecard-count                  INTEGER RANGE [1<=x<=100]  Number of LLM-generated cases when │
│                                                               --scorecard is set (1-100).        │
│                                                               Ignored otherwise.                 │
│                                                               [default: 10]                      │
│ --scorecard-mix                    TEXT                       Test-case mix when --scorecard is  │
│                                                               set: standard | edge | adversarial │
│                                                               | domain. Ignored otherwise.       │
│                                                               [default: standard]                │
│ --scorecard-judge-model            TEXT                       Override the LLM judge             │
│                                                               provider/model for the 10-category │
│                                                               rubric when --scorecard is set.    │
│                                                               Defaults to the agent's own model. │
│ --help                                                        Show this message and exit.        │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk eval-gen`

```

 Usage: mdk eval-gen [OPTIONS] AGENT

 Generate eval dataset entries for an agent via LLM.

 Each generated entry is ``{"input": {...}, "expected": {...},
 "generated": true}``. The ``expected`` field is the agent's
 ACTUAL response — review + edit if the current behavior isn't
 yet correct. Generated entries are flagged so a future
 mdk eval --strict can distinguish them.

 Examples:

   $ mdk eval-gen triage --num 20
   $ mdk eval-gen triage --num 5 --sample-input '{"text": "x"}'
   $ mdk eval-gen triage --num 10 -o evals/triage/cases.jsonl
   $ mdk eval-gen triage --num 3 --mock     # offline test
   $ mdk eval-gen triage --num 5 --mode adversarial  # red-team
   $ mdk eval-gen triage --num 5 --mode refusal      # refusal cases
   $ mdk eval-gen --guided                  # interactive wizard
   $ mdk eval-gen --all --num 10 --mock     # sweep every agent

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│   name      AGENT  Agent name (resolved under agents/<name>) or a literal path to an agent       │
│                    directory. Omit with --guided to pick interactively, or with --all to sweep   │
│                    every agent in the project.                                                   │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --num              -n                          INTEGER  How many cases to generate. Default 10;  │
│                                                         max 200.                                 │
│                                                         [default: 10]                            │
│ --guided           -g                                   Interactive wizard: walks the operator   │
│                                                         through agent selection, case count,     │
│                                                         provider (mock/real), and sample-input   │
│                                                         strategy — then runs the generator.      │
│                                                         Auto-triggered when mdk eval-gen is      │
│                                                         invoked with no agent from a TTY inside  │
│                                                         a project.                               │
│ --all                                                   Sweep every agent under ./agents/ in the │
│                                                         current project, generating --num cases  │
│                                                         for each. Skips agents that already have │
│                                                         a generated dataset unless --force is    │
│                                                         passed. Emits mdk_eval_gen_all_summary:  │
│                                                         for CI scrapers.                         │
│ --sample-input                                 TEXT     A reference input (JSON object) to bias  │
│                                                         generation. Useful when you want cases   │
│                                                         similar to a known good example.         │
│ --output           -o                          TEXT     Where to write the JSONL. Default:       │
│                                                         evals/<agent>/dataset.generated.jsonl    │
│                                                         under the project root.                  │
│ --mock                                                  Use MockProvider + synthetic             │
│                                                         schema-walking inputs — no LLM call.     │
│                                                         Useful for tests / offline /             │
│                                                         sanity-checking the schema before paying │
│                                                         for tokens.                              │
│ --with-dimensions      --no-with-dimensions             Annotate each entry with grounding       │
│                                                         (one-sentence context) and               │
│                                                         expected_coverage (2-4 topic slugs) via  │
│                                                         a second LLM call. These fields activate │
│                                                         faithfulness and coverage scoring in mdk │
│                                                         eval. Pass --no-with-dimensions to skip  │
│                                                         the extra call and generate              │
│                                                         accuracy-only entries.                   │
│                                                         [default: with-dimensions]               │
│ --mode             -m                          TEXT     Generation mode. Controls what kind of   │
│                                                         inputs the LLM produces:                 │
│                                                         standard   Diverse, realistic end-user   │
│                                                         inputs (default). adversarial            │
│                                                         Prompt-injection and policy-bypass       │
│                                                         attempts. edge        Boundary           │
│                                                         conditions: empty, very long, unusual    │
│                                                         chars. refusal     Inputs the agent      │
│                                                         should decline. Entries are tagged       │
│                                                         refusal_expected: true for the           │
│                                                         D-dimension gate.                        │
│                                                         Valid values: standard, adversarial,     │
│                                                         edge, refusal.                           │
│                                                         [default: standard]                      │
│ --force            -f                                   Overwrite OUTPUT if it already exists.   │
│ --yes              -y                                   Skip the confirmation prompt between     │
│                                                         Phase 1 (input generation) and Phase 2   │
│                                                         (agent execution). The prompt is also    │
│                                                         skipped automatically when stdin is not  │
│                                                         a TTY (e.g. CI pipelines).               │
│ --target-dim                                   TEXT     Bias generation toward a 10-category     │
│                                                         dimension. Repeatable. When set, the     │
│                                                         generator's prompt nudges it toward      │
│                                                         cases that specifically stress the named │
│                                                         dim(s) under the eval engine's scoring.  │
│                                                         Valid: task_success, accuracy,           │
│                                                         faithfulness, safety, completeness,      │
│                                                         tool_usage, workflow_adherence,          │
│                                                         consistency, latency, ux_tone. Example:  │
│                                                         --target-dim safety --target-dim         │
│                                                         faithfulness.                            │
│ --help                                                  Show this message and exit.              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk eval-generate`

```

 Usage: mdk eval-generate [OPTIONS] AGENT

 Author an eval dataset from a plain-English agent description.

 Review-then-commit: this command DOES NOT modify the
 agent's dataset on disk. It prints a summary so you can review,
 then quotes the mdk eval-generate-commit line to run
 next.

 Examples:

   $ mdk eval-generate triage --from "triages tickets" --count 30

   $ mdk eval-generate triage --from "..." --include-judge \
         --budget-usd 0.50 --target dev

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    agent      TEXT  Agent name (matches agent.yaml's `name`). [required]                       │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *  --from                   TEXT                       Plain-English agent description Claude    │
│                                                        will use to author the cases.             │
│                                                        [required]                                │
│    --count          -n      INTEGER RANGE [1<=x<=100]  How many cases. [default: 20]             │
│    --categories             TEXT                       Comma-separated categories. Default: all  │
│                                                        three.                                    │
│                                                        [default: happy,edge,adversarial]         │
│    --include-judge                                     Also draft a judge.yaml rubric.           │
│    --model                  TEXT                       Optional LiteLLM model string. Default:   │
│                                                        the agent's declared model.               │
│    --budget-usd             FLOAT                      Hard server-side cost ceiling.            │
│    --target                 TEXT                       Named target from your user-config.       │
│                                                        Default: MDK_RUNTIME_URL env var.         │
│    --json                                              Emit one JSON line per SSE event + the    │
│                                                        final summary as JSON.                    │
│    --help                                              Show this message and exit.               │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk eval-generate-commit`

```

 Usage: mdk eval-generate-commit [OPTIONS] AGENT JOB_ID

 Commit selected generated cases to the agent's dataset.

 The only mutation step in the generator flow — appends accepted
 cases to ``<agents_path>/<agent>/evals/dataset.jsonl`` on the
 target runtime.

 Examples:

   $ mdk eval-generate-commit triage evgen_abc123    # commit all

   $ mdk eval-generate-commit triage evgen_abc123 --cases c1,c3,c5

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    agent       TEXT  Agent name (matches the generate-step argument). [required]               │
│ *    job_id      TEXT  The ``evgen_*`` job id from the generate step. [required]                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --cases               TEXT  Comma-separated case ids to commit (e.g. c1,c3,c5). Default: commit  │
│                             every case in the job.                                               │
│ --commit-judge              Also write the drafted judge.yaml.                                   │
│ --target              TEXT  Named target.                                                        │
│ --json                      JSON output.                                                         │
│ --help                      Show this message and exit.                                          │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk eval-harvest`

```

 Usage: mdk eval-harvest [OPTIONS] AGENT

 Harvest prod runs into proposed eval cases (ADR 016 D1).

 Examples:

   # Propose cases from thumbs-down runs → evals/harvested.jsonl
   $ mdk eval harvest rag-qa

   # Golden cases from thumbs-up runs, to stdout
   $ mdk eval harvest rag-qa --source thumbs-up -o -

   # Review, then explicitly append to the live dataset
   $ mdk eval harvest rag-qa --source low-score --accept

 By default this NEVER modifies evals/dataset.jsonl — it writes a review
 file. Pass --accept to append the proposals to the live
 dataset (the deliberate human-review gate).

╭─ Arguments ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ *    agent      TEXT  Agent directory OR bare name (resolved to ./agents/<name> inside a         │
│                       project). Its evals/ folder is where the review file is written and where  │
│                       the live dataset.jsonl lives.                                              │
│                       [required]                                                                 │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --source          TEXT                   Which prod signal selects candidate runs: thumbs-down   │
│                                          (cases to fix) | thumbs-up (golden cases) | low-score | │
│                                          sample (signal-agnostic).                               │
│                                          [default: thumbs-down]                                  │
│ --limit   -n      INTEGER RANGE [x>=0]   Maximum number of proposed cases to harvest.            │
│                                          [default: 20]                                           │
│ --since           TEXT                   ISO-8601 timestamp; only consider runs/feedback at or   │
│                                          after this instant (e.g. 2026-05-01). Omit for no       │
│                                          cutoff.                                                 │
│ --output  -o      PATH                   Write the proposed cases (JSONL) here. Defaults to      │
│                                          <agent>/evals/harvested.jsonl. Use - for stdout.        │
│                                          Ignored when --accept is set.                           │
│ --accept                                 APPEND the proposed cases to the live                   │
│                                          <agent>/evals/dataset.jsonl. This is the explicit       │
│                                          human-gate step — without it, harvesting only proposes  │
│                                          and never mutates the dataset.                          │
│ --format          [table|json|markdown]  Summary output format. [default: table]                 │
│ --help                                   Show this message and exit.                             │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯

```

### `mdk eval-schedule`

```

 Usage: mdk eval-schedule [OPTIONS] COMMAND [ARGS]...

 Manage continuous-eval cadences per agent (ADR 016 D2).

╭─ Options ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ --help          Show this message and exit.                                                      │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
╭─ Commands ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
│ set     Set (or update) an agent's continuous-eval cadence.                                      │
│ list    List this project's continuous-eval schedules.                                           │
│ clear   Remove an agent's continuous-eval schedule.                                              │
╰──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╯
